Abstract: The concept of a security index quantifies the minimum number of components that must be compromised to carry out an undetectable attack. This metric enables system operators to quantify each component's security risk and implement countermeasures. In this paper, we introduce a data-driven security index that can be computed solely from input/output data when the system model is unknown. We show a sufficient condition under which the data-driven security index coincides with the model-based security index, which implies that the exact risk level of each component can be identified solely from the data. We provide an algorithm for computing the data-driven security index. Although computing this index is NP-hard, we derive a polynomial-time computable upper bound. ### [245] [No Cords Attached: Coordination-Free Concurrent Lock-Free Queues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09410)
*Yusuf Motiwala*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Cyclic Memory Protection (CMP) 是一种新型无锁队列，它通过有限的保护窗口提供实际的内存回收保证，解决了现有无锁队列在并发环境下过于复杂的问题。CMP 在保持严格 FIFO 语义、无界容量和无锁运行的同时，显著提高了性能和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无锁队列在并发环境下由于需要处理 ABA、使用后释放和不安全回收等问题，其复杂性远超普通队列，并且常常牺牲 FIFO 顺序、无界容量或无锁运行。AI 时代的高并发需求使得这些开销尤为突出，催生了对更简单、更高效的并发队列的需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Cyclic Memory Protection (CMP) 的新方法，通过引入有限的保护窗口来提供实际的内存回收保证，从而在不牺牲严格 FIFO 语义、无界容量和无锁运行的前提下，恢复了队列设计的简洁性。

Result: CMP 队列在内存回收方面提供了严格的 FIFO 顺序和安全性保证。实验表明，在髙并发场景下，CMP 的性能最高可达现有无锁队列的 1.72-4 倍，并且能够扩展到数百个线程，同时保持低开销。

Conclusion: CMP 证明了高并发队列可以回归其基本简洁性，同时不影响队列语义。通过有限的保护窗口，CMP 在保证安全性的同时，显著提高了并发队列的性能和可扩展性，满足了 AI 时代的需求。

Abstract: The queue is conceptually one of the simplest data structures-a basic FIFO container. However, ensuring correctness in the presence of concurrency makes existing lock-free implementations significantly more complex than their original form. Coordination mechanisms introduced to prevent hazards such as ABA, use-after-free, and unsafe reclamation often dominate the design, overshadowing the queue itself. Many schemes compromise strict FIFO ordering, unbounded capacity, or lock-free progress to mask coordination overheads. Yet the true source of complexity lies in the pursuit of infinite protection against reclamation hazards--theoretically sound but impractical and costly. This pursuit not only drives unnecessary complexity but also creates a protection paradox where excessive protection reduces system resilience rather than improving it. While such costs may be tolerable in conventional workloads, the AI era has shifted the paradigm: training and inference pipelines involve hundreds to thousands of concurrent threads per node, and at this scale, protection and coordination overheads dominate, often far heavier than the basic queue operations themselves.
  This paper introduces Cyclic Memory Protection (CMP), a coordination-free queue that preserves strict FIFO semantics, unbounded capacity, and lock-free progress while restoring simplicity. CMP reclaims the strict FIFO that other approaches sacrificed through bounded protection windows that provide practical reclamation guarantees. We prove strict FIFO and safety via linearizability and bounded reclamation analysis, and show experimentally that CMP outperforms state-of-the-art lock-free queues by up to 1.72-4x under high contention while maintaining scalability to hundreds of threads. Our work demonstrates that highly concurrent queues can return to their fundamental simplicity without weakening queue semantics.

</details>


### [246] [Distribution and Management of Datacenter Load Decoupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08936)
*Liuzixuan Lin,Andrew A. Chien*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: AI和云数据中心的功耗问题日益严重，这加剧了其碳足迹的长期担忧。数据中心灵活性（即负载适应）对于减少数据中心碳排放和提高电网可再生能源吸收能力至关重要。通过分离数据中心的电力容量和电网负载，可以实现数据中心灵活性，而无需干扰数据中心容量。该研究探讨了如何最佳地分配和管理这种分离，以最大限度地提高所有参与者的效益，并考虑了场地差异和数据中心-电网合作等关键因素。通过评估，研究表明优化的分配可以实现超过98%的潜在电网碳减排，而仅需满足70%的总分离需求。在管理方面，数据中心-电网合作（双向共享和控制与单向信息共享相比）可实现1.4倍的电网碳减排。最后，研究表明分离可能具有经济可行性，因为数据中心获得的电力成本和碳排放效益平均而言大于其本地分离成本。然而，不同场地之间的差异表明可能需要电网干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI和云数据中心的电力消耗急剧增长，引发了对其碳足迹的担忧。数据中心灵活性对于解决这一问题至关重要，因为它有助于提高电网对可再生能源的吸收能力。

Method: 研究人员定义并计算了数据中心负载分离所需的电力和能量，然后评估了设计的分配和管理方法。

Result: 优化的分配方法可以实现超过98%的潜在电网碳减排，而仅需70%的分离需求。数据中心-电网合作可实现1.4倍的电网碳减排。平均而言，数据中心从分离中获得的效益大于其成本。

Conclusion: 数据中心灵活性可以通过优化分配和管理策略来有效减少碳排放，并可能具有经济效益。然而，不同场地之间的差异可能需要电网干预。

Abstract: The exploding power consumption of AI and cloud datacenters (DCs) intensifies the long-standing concerns about their carbon footprint, especially because DCs' need for constant power clashes with volatile renewable generation needed for grid decarbonization. DC flexibility (a.k.a. load adaptation) is a key to reducing DC carbon emissions by improving grid renewable absorption.
  DC flexibility can be created, without disturbing datacenter capacity by decoupling a datacenter's power capacity and grid load with a collection of energy resources. Because decoupling can be costly, we study how to best distribute and manage decoupling to maximize benefits for all. Key considerations include site variation and datacenter-grid cooperation.
  We first define and compute the power and energy needs of datacenter load decoupling, and then we evaluate designed distribution and management approaches. Evaluation shows that optimized distribution can deliver >98% of the potential grid carbon reduction with 70% of the total decoupling need. For management, DC-grid cooperation (2-way sharing and control vs. 1-way info sharing) enables 1.4x grid carbon reduction. Finally, we show that decoupling may be economically viable, as on average datacenters can get power cost and carbon emissions benefits greater than their local costs of decoupling. However, skew across sites suggests grid intervention may be required.

</details>

*Jay Tharwani,Shobhit Aggarwal,Arnab A Purkayastha*

TL;DR: AWS在CPU性能上表现最佳，但价格昂贵；OCI成本最低，但性能稍逊；Azure和GCP表现居中，GCP的AMD实例有优势，但ARM实例性价比低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估云基础设施中高性能计算（HPC）风格的CPU性能和成本，重点关注AWS、Azure、GCP和OCI这四家主要云服务提供商，并在Intel、AMD和ARM的通用实例类型上，对比了按需和一年期折扣两种定价模式。

Result: AWS在所有实例类型中运行时长最短，但价格最高。OCI在所有CPU系列中成本最低，但运行时长通常比AWS慢。Azure的性能和成本通常居中。GCP在Intel和AMD实例之间性能有显著提升，但其ARM实例比其AMD实例慢一倍以上，且价格昂贵。AWS的内部数据显示，其ARM实例在运行时长上可比其Intel和AMD实例快49%。

Conclusion: 云实例的选择和提供商的选择会对运行时长和价格产生巨大影响，用户应根据工作负载的优先级（原始速度或成本最小化）来决定实例类型。

Abstract: This paper evaluates HPC-style CPU performance and cost in virtualized cloud infrastructures using a subset of OpenMP workloads in the SPEC ACCEL suite. AWS consistently delivers the shortest runtime in all three instance types, yet charges a premium, especially for on-demand usage. OCI emerges as the most economical option across all CPU families, although it generally runs workloads more slowly than AWS. Azure often exhibits mid-range performance and cost, while GCP presents a mixed profile: it sees a notable boost when moving from Intel to AMD. On the other hand, its ARM instance is more than twice as slow as its own AMD offering and remains significantly more expensive. AWS's internal comparisons reveal that its ARM instance can outperform its Intel and AMD siblings by up to 49 percent in runtime. These findings highlight how instance choices and provider selection can yield substantial variations in both runtime and price, indicating that workload priorities, whether raw speed or cost minimization, should guide decisions on instance types.

Result: 本文提出了一个企业级、隐私保护的联邦学习框架的设计愿景，该框架旨在解决当前 FL 框架在可扩展性、易用性和隐私保护方面存在的挑战。该框架具备本地模拟、无缝部署、跨异构基础设施的分布式部署、多级抽象以及全面的隐私和安全保护能力，能够有效地弥合研究原型与企业规模部署之间的差距。

Conclusion: 本文提出的企业级、隐私保护的联邦学习框架愿景，旨在通过提供一套全面的关键能力和灵活的架构设计，克服在科学领域部署可扩展、可靠且隐私保护的 AI 所面临的挑战，从而加速联邦学习在各行业的应用和发展。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) is a promising approach to enabling collaborative model training without centralized data sharing, a crucial requirement in scientific domains where data privacy, ownership, and compliance constraints are critical. However, building user-friendly enterprise-level FL frameworks that are both scalable and privacy-preserving remains challenging, especially when bridging the gap between local prototyping and distributed deployment across heterogeneous client computing infrastructures. In this paper, based on our experiences building the Advanced Privacy-Preserving Federated Learning (APPFL) framework, we present our vision for an enterprise-grade, privacy-preserving FL framework designed to scale seamlessly across computing environments. We identify several key capabilities that such a framework must provide: (1) Scalable local simulation and prototyping to accelerate experimentation and algorithm design; (2) seamless transition from simulation to deployment; (3) distributed deployment across diverse, real-world infrastructures, from personal devices to cloud clusters and HPC systems; (4) multi-level abstractions that balance ease of use and research flexibility; and (5) comprehensive privacy and security through techniques such as differential privacy, secure aggregation, robust authentication, and confidential computing. We further discuss architectural designs to realize these goals. This framework aims to bridge the gap between research prototypes and enterprise-scale deployment, enabling scalable, reliable, and privacy-preserving AI for science.

However, MIG's hardware rigidity and the conventional one-to-one allocation model jointly lead to severe fragmentation and cluster-wide underutilization. We present Flex-MIG, a software-only framework that replaces one-to-one with a one-to-many allocation model and enables host-shared-memory collectives across MIG instances without hardware modification. Flex-MIG eliminates drain-required reconfiguration, reduces fragmentation, and improves makespan by up to 17% across diverse traces, showing that rethinking MIG's operational model as a software-coordinated layer substantially improves cluster efficiency.

### [250] [Minimize Your Critical Path with Combine-and-Exchange Locks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09194)
*Simon König,Lukas Epple,Christian Becker*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 状态同步通过Combine-and-Exchange Scheduling (CES)在用户空间得到优化，性能提升显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有用户空间同步原语模仿内核级调度，在协程等用户空间调度的场景下引入了不必要的延迟，限制了吞吐量。

Method: 提出Combine-and-Exchange Scheduling (CES)调度方法，该方法确保受争用的关键代码段保持在同一执行线程上，同时将可并行化的工作均匀分布在其余线程上。

Result: CES在应用程序基准测试中实现了3倍性能提升，在微基准测试中实现了8倍性能提升。该方法易于应用于现有语言和库。

Conclusion: CES是一种新颖的调度方法，能够有效优化用户空间调度的同步性能，并已在实际应用中得到验证。

Abstract: Coroutines are experiencing a renaissance as many modern programming languages support the use of cooperative multitasking for highly parallel or asynchronous applications. One of the greatest advantages of this is that concurrency and synchronization is manged entirely in the userspace, omitting heavy-weight system calls. However, we find that state-of-the-art userspace synchronization primitives approach synchronization in the userspace from the perspective of kernel-level scheduling. This introduces unnecessary delays on the critical path of the application, limiting throughput. In this paper, we re-think synchronization for tasks that are scheduled entirely in the userspace (e.g., coroutines, fibers, etc.). We develop Combine-and-Exchange Scheduling (CES), a novel scheduling approach that ensures contended critical sections stay on the same thread of execution while parallelizable work is evenly spread across the remaining threads. We show that our approach can be applied to many existing languages and libraries, resulting in 3-fold performance improvements in application benchmarks as well as 8-fold performance improvements in microbenchmarks.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为SPADA的新编程语言，它提供了对数据放置、数据流模式和异步操作的精确控制，同时抽象了特定架构的底层细节。此外，还设计了一个严格的数据流语义框架来定义路由的正确性、数据竞争和死锁，并实现了一个针对Cerebras CSL的多级编译工具。

Abstract: Spatial dataflow architectures like the Cerebras Wafer-Scale Engine achieve exceptional performance in AI and scientific applications by leveraging distributed memory across processing elements (PEs) and localized computation. However, programming these architectures remains challenging due to the need for explicit orchestration of data movement through reconfigurable networks-on-chip and asynchronous computation triggered by data arrival. Existing FPGA and CGRA programming models emphasize loop scheduling but overlook the unique capabilities of spatial dataflow architectures, particularly efficient dataflow over regular grids and intricate routing management.
  We present SPADA, a programming language that provides precise control over data placement, dataflow patterns, and asynchronous operations while abstracting architecture-specific low-level details. We introduce a rigorous dataflow semantics framework for SPADA that defines routing correctness, data races, and deadlocks. Additionally, we design and implement a compiler targeting Cerebras CSL with multi-level lowering.
  SPADA serves as both a high-level programming interface and an intermediate representation for domain-specific languages (DSLs), which we demonstrate with the GT4Py stencil DSL. SPADA enables developers to express complex parallel patterns -- including pipelined reductions and multi-dimensional stencils -- in 6--8x less code than CSL with near-ideal weak scaling across three orders of magnitude. By unifying programming for spatial dataflow architectures under a single model, SPADA advances both the theoretical foundations and practical usability of these emerging high-performance computing platforms.

### [254] [Dynamic and Static Energy Efficient Design of Pinching Antenna Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08720)
*Saba Asaad,Chongjun Ouyang,Ali Bereyhi,Zhiguo Ding*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Pinch-antenna系统（PASSs）的能量效率，提出了一种计算功率分配的通用方法，并通过实验证明了动态调整天线耦合参数可显著提高系统能效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于PASSs的功率分配并非由功率分配策略直接控制，而是通过调整天线耦合和位置间接实现，因此需要研究新的功率分配方法以优化系统性能。

Method: 提出了一种计算PASSs中功率分配的通用方法。开发了一种混合动态-静态算法，通过以不同速率更新系统参数来最大化能量效率。

Result: 实验结果表明，动态调整天线耦合参数可以显著提高PASSs的能量效率。

Conclusion: 混合动态-静态算法是一种有效提高PASSs能量效率的方法，其中动态调整天线耦合参数尤为重要。

Abstract: We study the energy efficiency of pinching-antenna systems (PASSs) by developing a consistent formulation for power distribution in these systems. The per-antenna power distribution in PASSs is not controlled explicitly by a power allocation policy, but rather implicitly through tuning of pinching couplings and locations. Both these factors are tunable: (i) pinching locations are tuned using movable elements, and (ii) couplings can be tuned by varying the effective coupling length of the pinching elements. While the former is feasible to be addressed dynamically in settings with low user mobility, the latter cannot be addressed at a high rate. We thus develop a class of hybrid dynamic-static algorithms, which maximize the energy efficiency by updating the system parameters at different rates. Our experimental results depict that dynamic tuning of pinching locations can significantly boost energy efficiency of PASSs.

</details>

Existing software is developed based on models or motion-captured data, resulting in limited flexibility. Both computer vision and radar modules are included in the simulator. In computer vision module, the real-time model for object detection with global nearest neighbor is first used to detect and track human targets in the video. Then, the high-resolution network is used to estimate two-dimensional poses of the detected human targets. Next, the three-dimensional poses of the detected human targets are obtained by nearest matching method. Then, range-time map is generated using pulse compression, moving target indication, and DnCNN. Next, Doppler-time map (DTM) is generated using short-time Fourier transform and DnCNN again. Finally, the ridge features on the DTM are extracted using the maximum local energy method. In addition, a hybrid parallel-serial neural network architecture is proposed for radar-based HAR. Numerical experiments are conducted and analyzed to demonstrate the effectiveness of the designed simulator and the proposed network model. The open-source code of this work can be found in: https://github.com/JoeyBGOfficial/RadHARSimulatorV2-Video-to-Doppler-Generator.

### [263] [LMMSE-Optimal Pilot Pattern Design Based on Covariance Matrix Approximation for OFDM Channel Estimation in Doubly Dispersive Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09140)
*Xuyao Yu,Zijun Gong,Zhilu Lai*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本篇论文研究了OFDM系统中双重分频信道的最优导频模式设计，以线性最小均方误差（LMMSE）估计为基础。通过将信道协方差矩阵分解为延迟和多普勒域的厄米特托普利兹矩阵的克罗内克积，并利用Szegö极限定理，证明了这些矩阵近似可由离散傅里叶变换（DFT）矩阵对角化。基于此结构，LMMSE信道估计误差被重构为紧凑的解析形式，并推导出了一个闭式下界。此外，论文还确定了基于格子（lattice-based）的导频模式能够达到该下界的条件，并通过数值结果验证了矩阵近似的误差很小，并给出了所提出的格子设计示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本篇论文旨在解决OFDM系统中双重分频信道的导频模式设计问题，以期在LMMSE估计框架下实现最优的信道估计。

Method: 首先，将信道协方差矩阵分解为延迟和多普勒域的厄米特托普利兹矩阵的克罗内克积。然后，利用Szegö极限定理，证明这些矩阵近似可由DFT矩阵对角化。最后，基于此结构推导出LMMSE信道估计误差的紧凑解析形式和闭式下界，并确定了格子导频模式达到该下界的条件。

Result: 推导出了LMMSE信道估计误差的紧凑解析形式和闭式下界。证明了格子导频模式能够达到该下界的条件。数值结果表明，所提出的矩阵近似方法引入的误差很小。

Conclusion: 本研究成功设计了OFDM系统中双重分频信道的LMMSE最优导频模式，并通过理论和数值分析验证了所提出方法的有效性。

Abstract: This paper investigates the optimal pilot pattern design, in the linear minimum mean square error (LMMSE) estimator sense, for OFDM systems in doubly dispersive channels. To enable analytical tractability, the channel covariance matrix is decomposed into the Kronecker product of two Hermitian Toeplitz matrices corresponding to the delay and Doppler domains. By invoking the Szegö limit theorem, these matrices are shown to be approximately diagonalizable by discrete Fourier transform (DFT) matrices. Based on this structure, the LMMSE channel estimation error is reformulated into a compact analytical form, from which a closed-form lower bound is derived. Furthermore, we establish the condition under which this bound is achieved by a lattice-based pilot pattern. Numerical results verify that the proposed matrix approximation introduces negligible error and examples of the proposed lattice design are given.

### [264] [Mip-NeWRF: Enhanced Wireless Radiance Field with Hybrid Encoding for Channel Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09150)
*Yulin Fu,Jiancun Fan,Shiyu Zhai,Zhibo Duan,Jie Luo*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: Mip-NeWRF是一个基于物理信息约束的神经网络框架，用于在复杂室内环境中进行稀疏无线电测量下的精确信道预测。该方法通过引入多层感知机（MLP）、锥形 frustum 采样、尺度一致的混合位置编码以及课程学习策略，显著提高了信道预测的鲁棒性、收敛速度和准确性，并将NMSE降低了14.3 dB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的无线电场方法在复杂环境中用于信道预测时，鲁棒性、收敛速度和准确性均存在不足，需要更精细化的建模来解决这些问题。

Method: Mip-NeWRF采用基于射线（ray-based）的流水线，并结合了粗到精的重要性采样。具体包括：对frustum进行采样并进行编码；使用共享的多层感知机（MLP）处理编码后的信息；将MLP的输出合成为信道频率响应（CFR）。在MLP输入之前，进行了锥形frustum采样，并对每个frustum应用了尺度一致的混合位置编码。该编码器同时考虑了尺度不变性和细节的空间精度。在训练过程中，采用了课程学习策略来稳定和加速MLP的收敛。在信道合成过程中，结合了MLP输出的虚拟发射器存在概率和幅度，以及模型化的路径损耗和表面交互衰减，以提高物理保真度和准确性。

Abstract: Recent work on wireless radiance fields represents a promising deep learning approach for channel prediction, however, in complex environments these methods still exhibit limited robustness, slow convergence, and modest accuracy due to insufficiently refined modeling. To address this issue, we propose Mip-NeWRF, a physics-informed neural framework for accurate indoor channel prediction based on sparse channel measurements. The framework operates in a ray-based pipeline with coarse-to-fine importance sampling: frustum samples are encoded, processed by a shared multilayer perceptron (MLP), and the outputs are synthesized into the channel frequency response (CFR). Prior to MLP input, Mip-NeWRF performs conical-frustum sampling and applies a scale-consistent hybrid positional encoding to each frustum. The scale-consistent normalization aligns positional encodings across scene scales, while the hybrid encoding supplies both scale-robust, low-frequency stability to accelerate convergence and fine spatial detail to improve accuracy. During training, a curriculum learning schedule is applied to stabilize and accelerate convergence of the shared MLP. During channel synthesis, the MLP outputs, including predicted virtual transmitter presence probabilities and amplitudes, are combined with modeled pathloss and surface interaction attenuation to enhance physical fidelity and further improve accuracy. Simulation results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach: in typical scenarios, the normalized mean square error (NMSE) is reduced by 14.3 dB versus state-of-the-art baselines.

</details>

Abstract: This paper adapts a Multiple-Model Coding (MMC) approach for sampled electrical signal waveforms to satisfy reconstructed signal quality constraints. In the proposed approach, the parametric model and the rate allocated to the first stage, as well as the residual compression method of the second stage and its associated rate, are jointly optimized to achieve a target distortion of the reconstructed signal. Three approaches are proposed. An exhaustive search serves as a baseline for comparison. Then, an approach involving a Golden Section search is exploited to determine the rate of the first stage with reduced complexity. Finally, rate-distortion models of the compression efficiency for each model in the first stage are employed to obtain a subset of promising models in the first stage and reduced-size search intervals for the rate selection in both stages. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed reduced-complexity MMC approach reduces the rate for a given distortion constraint compared to state-of-the-art solutions for VCS with equivalent complexity.

</details>

Conclusion: 时延-多普勒、啁啾和时序域中的调制方案比时频调制方案更适合具有大时延和多普勒扩展的双选择性信道。

Abstract: There is significant recent interest in designing new modulation schemes for doubly-selective channels with large delay and Doppler spreads, where legacy modulation schemes based on time-frequency signal representations do not perform well. In this paper, we develop a framework for analyzing such modulations using two characteristics -- non-selectivity and predictability -- which directly relate to the diversity and spectral efficiency that the modulations achieve. We show that modulations in the delay-Doppler, chirp and time-sequency domains are non-selective, predictable and equivalent to one another, whereas time-frequency modulations are selective and non-predictable.

### [277] [LLM Enabled Beam Training for Pinching Antenna Systems (PASS)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09453)
*Deqiao Gan,Xiaoxia Xu,Xiaohu Ge,Yuanwei Liu*

Main category: eess.SP

  <summary>Details</summary>

Then, the optimal transmit beamforming is obtained by maximum ratio transmission (MRT). 2) For multi-user case, a joint codebook generation and beam selection problem is formulated based on the system sum rate under the minimum mean square error (MMSE) transmit beamforming. The training labels for pinching beamforming are constructed by selecting the beam combination that maximizes system performance from each user's Top-S candidate beams. Based on pretrained Generative Pre-trained Transformers (GPTs), the LLM is trained in an end-to-end fashion to minimize the cross-entropy loss. Simulation results demonstrate that: i) For single-user case, the proposed LLM-enabled PASS attains over 95% Top-1 accuracy in beam selection and achieves 51.92% improvements in beamforming gains compared to conventional method. ii) For multi-user case, the proposed LLM-enabled PASS framework significantly outperforms both the LLM-based massive MIMO and conventional PASS beam training, achieving up to 57.14% and 33.33% improvements in sum rate, respectively.

### [281] [Minimal Regret Walras Equilibria for Combinatorial Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09021)
*Aloïs Duguet,Tobias Harks,Martin Schmidt,Julian Schwarz*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该论文引入了 Δ-regret 瓦尔拉斯均衡的概念，这是一种在多物品市场中实现市场出清、容量可行性以及玩家总 regret 达到 Δ 的定价和分配机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多物品市场中，需要一种能够平衡市场出清、容量可行性和玩家 regret 的定价和分配机制。

Method: 论文推导了 Δ-regret 均衡存在的充要条件，并将其与社会福利问题的对偶差距和整数差距联系起来。对于单调估值，推导出的条件一致，并完全刻画了可实现的 Δ-regret 均衡。对于一般估值，论文将问题与线性优化的敏感性理论联系起来，并利用线性规划最优值函数敏感性间隙来界定可实现的 regret。

Result: 论文建立了 Δ-regret 均衡存在的充要条件，并将其与社会福利问题的对偶差距和整数差距联系起来。论文还利用线性规划最优值函数敏感性间隙来界定可实现的 regret，并将近似算法用于计算低 regret 瓦尔拉斯均衡。

Conclusion: 该研究为多物品市场中的 Δ-regret 瓦尔拉斯均衡提供了理论基础和计算方法，并将 regret 概念与市场出清、容量可行性和优化问题中的差距联系起来。

Abstract: We consider combinatorial multi-item markets and propose the notion of a $Δ$-regret Walras equilibrium, which is an allocation of items to players and a set of item prices that achieve the following goals: prices clear the market, the allocation is capacity-feasible, and the players' strategies lead to a total regret of $Δ$. The regret is defined as the sum of individual player regrets measured by the utility gap with respect to the optimal item bundle given the prices. We derive necessary and sufficient conditions for the existence of $Δ$-regret equilibria, where we establish a connection to the duality gap and the integrality gap of the social welfare problem. For the special case of monotone valuations, the derived necessary and sufficient optimality conditions coincide and lead to a complete characterization of achievable $Δ$-regret equilibria. For general valuations, we establish an interesting connection to the area of sensitivity theory in linear optimization. We show that the sensitivity gap of the optimal-value function of two (configuration) linear programs with changed right-hand side can be used to establish a bound on the achievable regret. Finally, we use these general structural results to translate known approximation algorithms for the social welfare optimization problem into algorithms computing low-regret Walras equilibria. We also demonstrate how to derive strong lower bounds based on integrality and duality gaps but also based on NP-complexity theory.

</details>

*Zhendong Guo,Wenchao Bai,Jiahui Jin*

### [283] [Steering Noncooperative Games Through Conjecture Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09435)
*Francesco Morri,Hélène Le Cadre,David Salas,Didier Aussel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在动态非合作博弈中，玩家在选择策略前会推测其他玩家的反应，但这可能导致多个均衡或不理想的结果。现有的方法通常分别处理这些问题，例如通过对手建模和激励设计。

Method: 提出一个激励设计框架，协调者首先通过优化目标函数来计算均衡，然后将此均衡作为玩家的目标。在中心化设置中，协调者还优化推测以引导玩家达到目标。在去中心化设置中，玩家独立计算推测并根据个人目标更新策略。该框架利用推测来引导系统达到理想结果，并将博弈分解为独立的优化问题，以实现大规模设置中的高效计算和并行化。

Conclusion: 该框架为解决动态非合作博弈中的多重均衡和非理想结果问题提供了一种新颖的解决方案，并通过将博弈分解为独立优化问题，实现了大规模设置中的高效计算和并行化。其在经典博弈中的应用潜力得到了证明。

Abstract: In dynamic noncooperative games, each player makes conjectures about other players' reactions before choosing a strategy. However, resulting equilibria may be multiple and do not always lead to desirable outcomes. These issues are typically addressed separately, for example, through opponent modelling and incentive design. Drawing inspiration from conjectural variations games, we propose an incentive design framework in which a coordinator first computes an equilibrium by optimizing a predefined objective function, then communicates this equilibrium as a target for the players to reach. In a centralized setting, the coordinator also optimizes the conjectures to steer the players towards the target. In decentralized settings, players independently compute conjectures and update their strategies based on individual targets. We provide a guarantee of equilibrium existence in both cases. This framework uses conjectures not only to guide the system towards desirable outcomes but also to decouple the game into independent optimization problems, enabling efficient computation and parallelization in large-scale settings. We illustrate our theoretical results on classical representative noncooperative games, demonstrating its application potential.

Our findings reveal substantial variation in the restrictiveness of proportionality across instances, including previously unobserved high levels of restrictiveness in some real-world cases. ### [285] [High-quality nanostructured diamond membranes for nanoscale quantum sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08632)
*Alexander Pakpour Tabrizi,Artur Lozovoi,Sean Karg,Tecla Bottinelli Mondandon,Melody Leung,Kai-Hung Cheng,Nathalie P. de Leon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种低损伤的金刚石纳米加工方法，并结合拾取-放置转移技术，实现了浅层氮-空位（NV）量子传感器的制备及其与各种传感目标的集成，同时保持了NV中心的优异光学和自旋性质，并增强了光子效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在凝聚态和材料物理学中应用金刚石中的氮-空位（NV）中心作为纳米级量子传感器，需要将NV中心置于靠近传感目标的位置。然而，现有的金刚石刻蚀和离子束刻蚀方法会引入损伤，影响NV中心的性能。

Method: 研究人员开发了一种低损伤的金刚石纳米加工流程，并采用拾取-放置转移技术来集成NV传感器。

Result: 所提出的方法制备的金刚石纳米结构能够保持靠近表面的NV中心的优异光学和自旋相干性，实现了显著的光子增强，并且可以方便地集成到不同的传感目标上。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了一种低损伤的金刚石纳米加工和集成方法，为实现高性能的浅层NV中心量子传感器及其在多种传感应用中的集成提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Deploying nitrogen vacancy (NV) centers in diamond as nanoscale quantum sensors for condensed matter and materials physics requires placing the NV centers close to the sensing target. One solution is to fabricate diamond nanostructures and integrate them with materials and devices. However, diamond etching and ion milling can introduce subsurface damage and surface defects that degrade the charge stability and spin coherence of NV centers near the surface. Here we report a procedure for fabricating low-damage nanostructured diamond membranes, and we show that this fabrication scheme preserves the optical and spin properties of state-of-the-art shallow NV center quantum sensors, within nanometers of the diamond surface, while providing significant photonic enhancement. Furthermore, we demonstrate a pick-and-place transfer method, which enables integration with diverse sensing targets.

</details>


### [286] [Dephasing-induced Quantum Hall Criticality in the Quantum Anomalous Hall system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08635)
*Fei Yang,Dong E. Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 纯粹的退相干足以产生整数量子霍尔效应的临界性，无需弹性无序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战了静态无序是整数量子霍尔效应（包括量子化平台和平台-平台跃迁）的必需品的传统观点。

Method: 从 Keldysh 表述出发，推导了一个开放系统的非线性 σ 模型（NLSM），该模型具有拓扑 θ 项但没有库珀单元格扇区。

Result: 推导出的 NLSM 证明了非微扰瞬子仍然控制着 (σxx, σxy) 的两参数流。在退相干量子反常霍尔设置中评估 θ，预测了在 σxy=1/2 处存在量子霍尔临界点，该临界点具有非零的 σxx，这是在没有安德森局域化的整数量子霍尔能谱的特征。

Conclusion: 通过将退相干确立为通往霍尔临界性的独立途径，该框架重构了开放固态和冷原子平台中的平台物理学，并为非酉物质中的拓扑传输提供了实用的诊断方法。

Abstract: Conventional wisdom holds that static disorder is indispensable to the integer quantum Hall effect, underpinning both quantized plateaus and the plateau-plateau transition. We show that pure dephasing, without elastic disorder, is sufficient to generate the same $θ$ driven criticality. Starting from a Keldysh formulation, we derive an open system nonlinear $σ$ model (NL$σ$M) for class A with a topological $θ$ term but no Cooperon sector, and we demonstrate that nonperturbative instantons still govern a two parameter flow of $(σ_{xx},σ_{xy})$. Evaluating $θ$ in a dephasing quantum anomalous Hall setting, we predict a quantum Hall critical point at $σ_{xy}=1/2$ with finite $σ_{xx}$ the hallmark of the integer quantum Hall universality class realized without Anderson localization. Boundary driven simulations of the Qi_Wu_Zhang model with local dephasing confirm this prediction and provide an experimentally aligned protocol to extract $(σ_{xx},σ_{xy})$ from Hall potential maps. By establishing dephasing as a self contained route to Hall criticality, our framework reframes plateau physics in open solid state and cold atom platforms and offers practical diagnostics for topological transport in nonunitary matter.

</details>


### [287] [Mechanical and electrical properties of a nano-gap or how to play the nano-accordion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08727)
*Simon Hettler,Raul Arenal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 原位透射电子显微镜(TEM)可用于研究与电流相关的现象，本研究提出了一种新的原位TEM器件，用于分析特定错位层状化合物的晶体取向与(热)电性质之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究特定错位层状化合物的晶体取向与(热)电性质之间的关系。

Method: 使用原位透射电子显微镜(TEM)技术，并制备了一种特殊的原位TEM器件，该器件在晶界处形成纳米尺寸的间隙，可以通过施加差分加热电流来精确控制机械弯曲。

Result: 器件的(热)电性质受到间隙的显著影响，产生了高内禀电压，该电压还受到真空环境和施加加热电流历史的影响。

Conclusion: 内部表面（例如间隙中的吸附分子）即使在高真空条件下也能显著影响化合物的电学性质。

Abstract: In-situ transmission electron microscopy (TEM) has become an important technique to study dynamic processes at highest spatial resolution and one branch is the investigation of phenomena related with electrical currents. Here, we present experimental results obtained from a peculiar in-situ TEM device, which was prepared with the aim to analyze the relationship between (thermo)electric properties and specific crystal orientations of a misfit layered compound. The formation of a nano-sized gap at a grain boundary facilitated a precisely controllable mechanical bending of the device by application of differential heating currents. The devices' electrical properties were found to be substantially influenced by the gap, leading to a high intrinsic voltage. This voltage additionally depends on the vacuum environment and on the history of applied heating currents. These findings are largely attributed to the presence of adsorbed molecules within the gap region. The electrical in-situ TEM studies of this work illustrate that interior surfaces can strongly influence electrical properties even under high vacuum conditions.

</details>


### [288] [Dynamical Orbital Angular Momentum Induced by Chiral Phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09271)
*Dapeng Yao,Dongwook Go,Yuriy Mokrousov,Shuichi Murakami*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 手性声子动力学地诱导出电子的轨道角动量（OAM），源于电子获得贝里相的绝热演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索手性声子诱导电子OAM的机制，并将其应用于实际材料。

Method: 构建包含p轨道的蜂窝晶格紧束缚模型，模拟手性声子对电子轨道重叠的调制，并计算生成的OAM。随后，构建不同伪角动量的谷声子有效模型，识别其不同的谷间散射通道。

Result: 手性声子能够诱导电子产生OAM，其符号取决于声子的手性。提出的模型能够描述单层过渡金属硫属化合物中诱导的OAM，并揭示了晶格-OAM的直接传递机制。

Conclusion: 手性声子诱导的OAM为轨道电子学应用提供了一种新的有前景的途径。

Abstract: We show that the orbital angular momentum (OAM) of electrons is dynamically induced by chiral phonons. The induced OAM originates from the adiabatic evolution in which electrons dynamically acquire Berry phase. By introducing a tight-binding model with p orbitals on a honeycomb lattice, we show a microscopic picture that chiral phonons modulate orbital overlaps of electrons, and calculate the generated OAM, whose sign depends on phonon chirality. We then construct an effective model for valley phonons with different phonon pseudoangular momenta (PAM) and identity their distinct intervalley-scattering channels. Our model obeys the selection rule between phonons and electrons with the orbital degree of freedom. Extending this framework to d-orbital electrons, our model is applied to describe the induced OAM in monolayer transition metal dichalcogenides. Our results reveal a direct lattice-OAM transfer mechanism that emerges even in materials with weak spin-orbital coupling, opening a new promising way for orbitronics applications.

</details>


### [289] [Interface tuned Enhanced and Low Temperature Quenching of Orbital Hall Currents Induce Torque and magnetoresistance in Light Metal/Nickel Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09349)
*Dhananjaya Mahapatra,Harekrishna Bhunia,Manu S Pattelath,Partha Mitra*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了轻金属/铁磁金属双层结构中的轨道霍尔效应及其相关的轨道力矩和磁阻效应，并证明了这些效应主要源于体内的轨道霍尔效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究轻金属/铁磁金属双层结构中的轨道霍尔效应，以理解和量化轨道霍尔力矩（OHT）和单向轨道磁电阻（UOMR）。

Method: 通过测量施加交流电流下，钛/镍双层薄膜的二次谐波纵向和横向电压，并引入铜中间层进行对比研究，以及系统性地改变钛的厚度和温度，来提取OHT效率和UOMR。

Result: 在钛/镍双层结构中观察到了OHT和UOMR。在镍/钛界面插入铜层能增强OHT效率和UOMR。OHT效率和UOMR随钛层厚度增加而增加，表明效应主要源于钛的体相。降低温度会导致OHT效率和UOMR降低。

Conclusion: 轨道霍尔效应是驱动OHT和UOMR的主要机制，该效应主要存在于轻金属层（钛）的体相中，并且其效应与温度密切相关。

Abstract: We investigate orbital current induced effects arising from the orbital Hall effect in light-metal/ferromagnet bilayers. Thin films of Ti in ohmic contact with Ni were studied using second-harmonic longitudinal and transverse voltage measurements under an applied a.c. current. From these signals, we extract the orbital Hall torque (OHT) efficiency and the unidirectional orbital magnetoresistance (UOMR). Insertion of a Cu interlayer between the Ni/Ti interface leads to an enhancement of both OHT efficiency and UOMR compared to both Ni/Ti and Ni/Cu bilayers. Furthermore, systematic variation of Ti thickness reveals that both OHT efficiency and UOMR increase with increasing Ti thickness, indicating that the observed phenomena predominantly originate from the bulk orbital Hall effect rather than purely from interfacial mechanisms and Lowering the temperature leads to a clear reduction in both the orbital Hall torque (OHT) efficiency and the unidirectional orbital magnetoresistance (UOMR). The nearly linear and correlated temperature dependence of both parameters suggests a common underlying mechanism, namely, the orbital Hall effect in the light-metal layer, which governs both the generation of orbital current and its subsequent influence on the ferromagnet through orbital torque and orbital magnetoresistance.

</details>


### [290] [Spin and orbital-to-charge conversion in noncentrosymmetric materials: Hall versus Rashba-Edelstein effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09511)
*Diego Garcia Ovalle,Aurelien Manchon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究在非磁性材料中研究了自旋-电荷和轨道-电荷的相互转换现象，将霍尔效应和Rashba-Edelstein效应的贡献同等对待。我们基于宏观可观测量开发了一个通用的形式主义，并通过铁电GeTe的案例研究验证了该理论。我们发现，获得的有效Rashba参数比之前报道的该材料值要小。将这些参数纳入漂移-扩散模型，我们表明产生的电流主要由Rashba-Edelstein效应控制，而不是由自旋或轨道霍尔效应控制。我们的工作重新定义了自旋-电荷和轨道-电荷相互转换系数，使其能够通过直接可测量的可观测量来表示，并鼓励研究界重新审视其他缺乏反演对称性的量子材料中的这些过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在具有破坏的体反演对称性的非磁性材料中，自旋-轨道耦合相互转换中的霍尔效应和Rashba-Edelstein效应。

Method: 开发了一个基于宏观可观测量（例如霍尔系数和自旋霍尔效应）的通用理论形式主义，并将其应用于铁电GeTe材料。利用漂移-扩散模型来分析自旋-轨道-电荷转换效应。

Result: 在铁电GeTe材料中，发现有效的Rashba参数比先前报告的值要小。通过漂移-扩散模型，结果表明，由自旋-轨道相互转换产生的电荷流主要受Rashba-Edelstein效应的控制，而不是自旋霍尔效应或轨道霍尔效应。

Conclusion: 自旋-轨道-电荷相互转换系数可以根据宏观可观测量来重新定义。研究结果表明，在GeTe中，Rashba-Edelstein效应是电荷产生的主要机制。鼓励社区重新审视其他缺乏反演对称性的量子材料中的自旋-轨道-电荷相互转换过程。

Abstract: We investigate spin- and orbital-to-charge conversion phenomena in nonmagnetic materials with broken inversion symmetry, treating the contributions from the Hall effect and the Rashba-Edelstein effect on an equal footing. We develop a general formalism for this interconversion based solely on macroscopic observables. The theory is validated through a case study of ferroelectric GeTe, where we find that the effective Rashba parameter obtained is smaller than previously reported values for the same material. Incorporating these parameters into a drift-diffusion model, we show that the generated charge current is primarily governed by the Rashba-Edelstein effect, rather than by the spin or orbital Hall effects. Our work redefines the spin- and orbit-to-charge interconversion coefficients in terms of directly measurable observables, encouraging the community to revisit these processes in other quantum materials lacking inversion symmetry.

</details>


### [291] [Probing the features of electron dispersion by tunneling between slightly twisted bilayer graphene sheets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09550)
*Alexey A. Sokolik,Azat F. Aminov,Evgenii E. Vdovin,Yurii N. Khanin,Mikhail A. Kashchenko,Denis A. Bandurin,Davit A. Ghazaryan,Sergey V. Morozov,Kostya S. Novoselov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 在双层石墨烯(BLG)器件中，我们发现了电子-空穴不对称的能带结构和垂直电场引起的能隙打开现象，并通过理论模型进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究双层石墨烯(BLG)中的电子-空穴不对称能带结构和垂直电场对能隙的影响，以及这些现象对隧穿电导的影响。

Method: 通过测量两层BLG之间的隧穿电导，并建立理论模型来解释观察到的现象。

Result: 发现了电子-空穴不对称的能带结构，其中空穴隧穿电导因态密度较高而增强。还发现了垂直电场引起的能隙打开，导致隧穿共振的不对称性，以及隧穿电流对栅极电压的敏感性。

Conclusion: 理论模型能够很好地复现实验结果，证实了电子-空穴不对称能带结构和电场诱导的能隙打开是BLG中的关键现象。

Abstract: Tunneling conductance between two bilayer graphene (BLG) sheets separated by 2 nm-thick insulating barrier was measured in two devices with the twist angles between BLGs less than 1°. At small bias voltages, the tunneling occurs with conservation of energy and momentum at the points of intersection between two relatively shifted Fermi circles. Here, we experimentally found and theoretically described signatures of electron-hole asymmetric band structure of BLG: since holes are heavier, the tunneling conductance is enhanced at the hole doping due to the higher density of states. Another key feature of BLG that we explore is gap opening in a vertical electric field with a strong polarization of electron wave function at van Hove singularities near the gap edges. This polarization, by shifting electron wave function in one BLG closer to or father from the other BLG, gives rise to asymmetric tunneling resonances in the conductance around charge neutrality points, which result in strong sensitivity of the tunneling current to minor changes of the gate voltages. The observed phenomena are reproduced by our theoretical model taking into account electrostatics of the dual-gated structure, quantum capacitance effects, and self-consistent gap openings in both BLGs.

</details>

### [292] [A Simple Analysis of Ranking in General Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08801)
*Mahsa Derakhshan,Mohammad Roghani,Mohammad Saneian,Tao Yu*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: Ranking算法在一般图上可实现(1/2 + c)-近似匹配，其中c >= 0.005。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation:  KV V90 年开创性工作中引入的 Ranking 算法。

Method: 对 Ranking 算法进行简单的组合分析。

Result: Ranking算法在一般图上可实现(1/2 + c)-近似匹配，其中c >= 0.005。

Conclusion: Ranking算法在一般图上可实现(1/2 + c)-近似匹配。

Abstract: We provide a simple combinatorial analysis of the Ranking algorithm, originally introduced in the seminal work by Karp, Vazirani, and Vazirani [KVV90], demonstrating that it achieves a $(1/2 + c)$-approximate matching for general graphs for $c \geq 0.005$.

</details>


### [293] [Space-Efficient and Output-Sensitive Algorithms for the Longest Common Bitonic Subsequence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08958)
*Md. Tanzeem Rahat,Md. Manzurul Hasan*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: LCBS的二次动态规划的空间障碍并非固有的，我们可以通过细化的滚动行实现，在θ(nm)时间内，仅用θ(min(n,m))的额外内存来解决。通过将M个符号匹配及其C个双调兼容对分离出来，我们可以将LCBS转化为稀疏DAG中的最长路径问题，并在O((n+m)log n + M log M)时间内以O(M)的空间复杂度解决，这在M << nm时比二次基线具有渐进优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LCBS能模拟生物信息学、金融和信号分析中的升降模式，但之前的解决方案需要θ(nm)的时间和空间复杂度。

Method: 提出了一种细化的滚动行实现，将LCBS的计算内存从θ(nm)降低到θ(min(n,m))。通过将LCBS问题转化为稀疏有向无环图（DAG）中的最长路径问题，实现了更快的渐进时间复杂度。

Result: 该方法将LCBS的计算复杂度从θ(nm)降低到O((n+m)log n + M log M)时间，空间复杂度为O(M)，其中M是符号匹配的数量。这使得之前无法处理的大规模输入的LCBS计算成为可能。

Conclusion: LCBS的计算复杂度可以通过新的方法得到优化，将空间复杂度显著降低，并提供更快的渐进时间复杂度，使得LCBS在实际应用中更具可行性，并为进一步研究开辟了新的方向。

Abstract: The longest common bitonic subsequence (LCBS) of two sequences A and B is the longest subsequence that increases to a single peak and then decreases while appearing, in order, in both inputs. Although LCBS naturally models rise-fall patterns in bioinformatics, finance, and signal analysis, the only previously documented solution was a quadratic dynamic program that needs θ(nm) time and space. We show that this space barrier is not inherent: a refined rolling-row implementation evaluates the same recurrence in θ(nm) time with only θ(min(n, m)) additional memory. By isolating the M symbol matches and their C bitonic-compatible pairs, we cast LCBS as a longest-path problem in a sparse DAG and solve it in O((n + m) log n + M log M) time and O(M) space, which is asymptotically faster than the quadratic baseline whenever M << n m. These results make exact LCBS computation practical for inputs that were previously out of reach and expose a new fine-grained complexity landscape that invites further exploration.

</details>


### [294] [Prophet and Secretary at the Same Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09531)
*Gregory Kehne,Thomas Kesselheim*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本论文研究在线问题中的随机设置，特别是最优停止问题，并探讨了算法对分布错误指定的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在随机设置的在线问题中，输入要么来自已知分布，要么来自未知分布。这两种情况分别对应于已知的先知不等式和未知的秘书问题。本文旨在探讨是否存在一种停止规则，能够同时在先知不等式和秘书问题这两种设定下都表现出竞争力，即同时获得较好的近似比。

Method: 作者提出了一系列算法，能够在 i.i.d. 先知问题和秘书问题上同时获得非平凡的联合保证，并且是最优的。同时，作者也证明了一些理论上的不可能，确定了哪些联合近似比（α, β）是任何自适应停止规则都无法达到的。研究同时考虑了固定数量的到达（n arrivals）和泊松过程到达（Poisson process with rate n）两种情况，并主要在泊松设置下进行研究，同时提供了泊松和n次到达设置之间的归约方法。

Result: 作者引入了一类新的算法，能够同时处理先知问题和秘书问题，并给出了最优的联合近似比。此外，还证明了某些联合近似比是无法实现的。

Conclusion: 本研究为在线最优停止问题提供了新的见解，特别是在算法对分布假设的鲁棒性方面。研究结果不仅为先知问题和秘书问题同时提供了最优的解决方案，还确定了理论上的可行边界。

Abstract: Many online problems are studied in stochastic settings for which inputs are samples from a known distribution, given in advance, or from an unknown distribution. Such distributions model both beyond-worst-case inputs and, when given, partial foreknowledge for the online algorithm. But how robust can such algorithms be to misspecification of the given distribution? When is this detectable, and when does it matter? When can algorithms give good competitive ratios both when the input distribution is as specified, and when it is not?
  We consider these questions in the setting of optimal stopping, where the cases of known and unknown distributions correspond to the well-known prophet inequality and to the secretary problem, respectively. Here we ask: Can a stopping rule be competitive for the i.i.d. prophet inequality problem and the secretary problem at the same time? We constrain the Pareto frontier of simultaneous approximation ratios $(α, β)$ that a stopping rule can attain.
  We introduce a family of algorithms that give nontrivial joint guarantees and are optimal for the extremal i.i.d. prophet and secretary problems. We also prove impossibilities, identifying $(α, β)$ unattainable by any adaptive stopping rule. Our results hold for both $n$ fixed arrivals and for arrivals from a Poisson process with rate $n$. We work primarily in the Poisson setting, and provide reductions between the Poisson and $n$-arrival settings that may be of broader interest.

</details>

### [295] [3D Guard-Layer: An Integrated Agentic AI Safety System for Edge Artificial Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08842)
*Eren Kurshan,Yuan Xie,Paul Franzon*

Main category: cs.AR

Despite the implementation of guardrails and safety mechanisms, security vulnerabilities and challenges have become increasingly prevalent in this domain, posing a significant barrier to the practical deployment and safety of AI systems. This paper proposes an agentic AI safety architecture that leverages 3D to integrate a dedicated safety layer. It introduces an adaptive AI safety infrastructure capable of dynamically learning and mitigating attacks against the AI system. The system leverages the inherent advantages of co-location with the edge computing hardware to continuously monitor, detect and proactively mitigate threats to the AI system. ### [296] [FsimNNs: An Open-Source Graph Neural Network Platform for SEU Simulation-based Fault Injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09131)

Moreover, to further investigate the efficiency of the approach, we evaluate the predictive capability of STGNNs across multiple test cases and discuss their generalization capability. The developed platform and datasets are released as open-source to support reproducibility and further research on https://github.com/luli2021/FsimNNs.

### [297] [Stabilizing Direct Training of Spiking Neural Networks: Membrane Potential Initialization and Threshold-robust Surrogate Gradient](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08708)
*Hyunho Kook,Byeongho Yu,Jeong Min Oh,Eunhyeok Park*

Main category: cs.NE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent advancements in SNNs offer energy efficiency, but challenges like temporal covariate shift (TCS) and unstable gradient flow with learnable neuron thresholds hinder their training.

Method: MP-Init aligns initial membrane potential with its stationary distribution to address TCS. TrSG stabilizes gradient flow with respect to threshold voltage during training.

Result: The proposed approach achieves state-of-the-art accuracy on both static and dynamic image datasets.

Conclusion: The presented MP-Init and TrSG methods effectively address key training challenges in SNNs, leading to improved performance and enabling more efficient AI paradigms.

Abstract: Recent advancements in the direct training of Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) have demonstrated high-quality outputs even at early timesteps, paving the way for novel energy-efficient AI paradigms. However, the inherent non-linearity and temporal dependencies in SNNs introduce persistent challenges, such as temporal covariate shift (TCS) and unstable gradient flow with learnable neuron thresholds. In this paper, we present two key innovations: MP-Init (Membrane Potential Initialization) and TrSG (Threshold-robust Surrogate Gradient). MP-Init addresses TCS by aligning the initial membrane potential with its stationary distribution, while TrSG stabilizes gradient flow with respect to threshold voltage during training. Extensive experiments validate our approach, achieving state-of-the-art accuracy on both static and dynamic image datasets. The code is available at: https://github.com/kookhh0827/SNN-MP-Init-TRSG

### [298] [Tractable Weighted First-Order Model Counting with Bounded Treewidth Binary Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09174)
*Václav Kůla,Qipeng Kuang,Yuyi Wang,Yuanhong Wang,Ondřej Kuželka*

Main category: cs.LO

TL;DR: WFOMC在有界二阶变量片段和有界树宽证据下是可处理的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决条件WFOMC在证据下的计算困难问题，即使对于本身易处理的逻辑片段也是如此。

Method: 通过限制证据的Gaifman图具有有界树宽，提出针对二阶变量片段FO^2和C^2的有界树宽证据的WFOMC多项式时间算法。

Result: 开发出一种新的算法，能够处理有界树宽的二阶变量逻辑片段的条件WFOMC问题，并成功应用于解决有界度图上的稳定座位安排问题，解决了该领域的开放性难题。该算法的扩展性通过实验得到验证。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法为处理受限证据的WFOMC问题提供了一个有效的解决方案，并拓宽了其在组合优化问题中的应用范围。

Abstract: The Weighted First-Order Model Counting Problem (WFOMC) asks to compute the weighted sum of models of a given first-order logic sentence over a given domain. Conditioning WFOMC on evidence -- fixing the truth values of a set of ground literals -- has been shown impossible in time polynomial in the domain size (unless $\mathsf{\#P \subseteq FP}$) even for fragments of logic that are otherwise tractable for WFOMC without evidence. In this work, we address the barrier by restricting the binary evidence to the case where the underlying Gaifman graph has bounded treewidth. We present a polynomial-time algorithm in the domain size for computing WFOMC for the two-variable fragments $\text{FO}^2$ and $\text{C}^2$ conditioned on such binary evidence. Furthermore, we show the applicability of our algorithm in combinatorial problems by solving the stable seating arrangement problem on bounded-treewidth graphs of bounded degree, which was an open problem. We also conducted experiments to show the scalability of our algorithm compared to the existing model counting solvers.

</details>

### [299] [Practical and Performant Enhancements for Maximization of Algebraic Connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08694)
*Leonard Jung,Alan Papalia,Kevin Doherty,Michael Everett*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 我们改进了MAC图稀疏化算法，使其在长期图状态估计中更具可扩展性和实时性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图估计方法在处理大规模、长期图时效率低下。MAC算法虽然能保持估计性能，但计算成本高且需要手动预设边集，不适合在线使用。

Method: 1. 开发了专门的代数连通性求解器，使运行时间平均缩短一倍。2. 研究了MAC优化过程的高级步长策略，以提高收敛速度和解的质量。3. 提出了自动方案，无需手动指定边即可保证图的连通性。

Result: 改进后的MAC算法在可扩展性、可靠性以及适用于实时估计应用方面得到了提升。

Conclusion: 通过计算优化、高级步长策略和自动连通性保证，我们显著改进了MAC算法，使其能够更有效地处理大规模、长期图的状态估计问题。

Abstract: Long-term state estimation over graphs remains challenging as current graph estimation methods scale poorly on large, long-term graphs. To address this, our work advances a current state-of-the-art graph sparsification algorithm, maximizing algebraic connectivity (MAC). MAC is a sparsification method that preserves estimation performance by maximizing the algebraic connectivity, a spectral graph property that is directly connected to the estimation error. Unfortunately, MAC remains computationally prohibitive for online use and requires users to manually pre-specify a connectivity-preserving edge set. Our contributions close these gaps along three complementary fronts: we develop a specialized solver for algebraic connectivity that yields an average 2x runtime speedup; we investigate advanced step size strategies for MAC's optimization procedure to enhance both convergence speed and solution quality; and we propose automatic schemes that guarantee graph connectivity without requiring manual specification of edges. Together, these contributions make MAC more scalable, reliable, and suitable for real-time estimation applications.

</details>

This review identifies and connects key components enabling intuitive information exchange and skill transfer between humans and robots. ### [301] [ATOM-CBF: Adaptive Safe Perception-Based Control under Out-of-Distribution Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08741)
*Kai S. Yun,Navid Azizan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ATOM-CBF是一个新的安全控制框架，可以适应来自未见过（OoD）测量值的认知不确定性，而无需地面真实标签或有关分布变化的信息。该框架通过（1）一个 OoD 感知自适应误差范围和（2）一个安全过滤器（可根据自适应误差范围调整其保守性）来实现。该方法在模拟中得到验证，可用于 F1Tenth 车辆和四足机器人。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界系统，特别是那些依赖学习到的感知模块从高维传感器数据推断系统状态的系统，其安全性难以保证。这些感知模块容易出现认知不确定性，在遇到训练期间未见过的非分布内（OoD）测量时常常会失效。

Method: ATOM-CBF (Adaptive-To-OoD-Measurement Control Barrier Function) 框架通过两个关键组件来解决此问题：(1) 一个 OoD 感知自适应误差范围，(2) 一个集成此自适应误差范围的安全过滤器。该过滤器能够实时调整其保守性。

Result: 在模拟中，ATOM-CBF 成功地为使用 LiDAR 扫描的 F1Tenth 车辆和使用 RGB 图像的四足机器人维护了安全性。

Conclusion: ATOM-CBF 框架能够有效处理来自 OoD 测量值的认知不确定性，为现实世界系统的安全控制提供了一种新的解决方案。

Abstract: Ensuring the safety of real-world systems is challenging, especially when they rely on learned perception modules to infer the system state from high-dimensional sensor data. These perception modules are vulnerable to epistemic uncertainty, often failing when encountering out-of-distribution (OoD) measurements not seen during training. To address this gap, we introduce ATOM-CBF (Adaptive-To-OoD-Measurement Control Barrier Function), a novel safe control framework that explicitly computes and adapts to the epistemic uncertainty from OoD measurements, without the need for ground-truth labels or information on distribution shifts. Our approach features two key components: (1) an OoD-aware adaptive perception error margin and (2) a safety filter that integrates this adaptive error margin, enabling the filter to adjust its conservatism in real-time. We provide empirical validation in simulations, demonstrating that ATOM-CBF maintains safety for an F1Tenth vehicle with LiDAR scans and a quadruped robot with RGB images.

</details>


### [302] [CENIC: Convex Error-controlled Numerical Integration for Contact](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08771)
*Vince Kurtz,Alejandro Castro*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CENIC是一个连续时间积分器，它结合了凸时间步进和误差控制积分的优点，在保持高精度的同时，运行速度与当代的机器人模拟器相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人模拟器在离散时间下运行，需要用户选择时间步长，这既关键又困难。过大的时间步长可能导致物理模拟失真，而过小的时间步长则会降低模拟速度。现有的连续时间误差控制积分器难以处理接触动力学的刚性问题，并且无法满足现代机器人工作流的速度和可扩展性要求。

Method: 提出了一种名为CENIC的新型连续时间积分器，它结合了近期在凸时间步进和误差控制积分方面的进展。

Result: CENIC 运行速度快，接近 MuJoCo、Drake 和 Isaac Sim 等离散时间机器人模拟器的实时运行速率，同时还能保证精度和收敛性。

Conclusion: CENIC 解决了现有连续时间积分器在处理机器人模拟中的刚性动力学和速度要求方面的不足，能够满足机器人工作流的性能要求。

Abstract: State-of-the-art robotics simulators operate in discrete time. This requires users to choose a time step, which is both critical and challenging: large steps can produce non-physical artifacts, while small steps force the simulation to run slowly. Continuous-time error-controlled integration avoids such issues by automatically adjusting the time step to achieve a desired accuracy. But existing error-controlled integrators struggle with the stiff dynamics of contact, and cannot meet the speed and scalability requirements of modern robotics workflows. We introduce CENIC, a new continuous-time integrator that brings together recent advances in convex time-stepping and error-controlled integration, inheriting benefits from both continuous integration and discrete time-stepping. CENIC runs at fast real-time rates comparable to discrete-time robotics simulators like MuJoCo, Drake and Isaac Sim, while also providing guarantees on accuracy and convergence.

</details>


### [303] [Dual-Arm Whole-Body Motion Planning: Leveraging Overlapping Kinematic Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.08778)
*Richard Cheng,Peter Werner,Carolyn Matl*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 通过利用双臂机器人共享关节引入的结构，提出了新的运动规划方法，有效缓解了高维度配置空间的“维度灾难”，并在真实杂货店环境中实现了高效的实时规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高自由度双臂机器人在人类环境中操作的需求日益增长，但实时运动规划在未知、变化的环境中仍然是一个挑战，原因是配置空间维度高且碰撞避免约束复杂。

Method: 首先，为每个运动链（左臂+躯干，右臂+躯干）构建了两个具有由共享关节引起的特定结构的动态路线图（DRM）。然后，利用这种结构高效搜索两个路线图的组合，从而在很大程度上避免“维度灾难”。

Result: 在真实的杂货店环境中，针对一个19自由度的机器人执行杂货配送任务的运动规划器进行了多项实验，平均规划时间为0.4秒，在超过2000次运动规划中成功率达到99.9%。

Conclusion: 所提出的利用共享关节结构的新型运动规划方法，能够有效缓解高维度配置空间的“维度灾难”，并在真实世界的应用中取得了高效和高成功的运动规划。

Abstract: High degree-of-freedom dual-arm robots are becoming increasingly common due to their morphology enabling them to operate effectively in human environments. However, motion planning in real-time within unknown, changing environments remains a challenge for such robots due to the high dimensionality of the configuration space and the complex collision-avoidance constraints that must be obeyed. In this work, we propose a novel way to alleviate the curse of dimensionality by leveraging the structure imposed by shared joints (e.g. torso joints) in a dual-arm robot. First, we build two dynamic roadmaps (DRM) for each kinematic chain (i.e. left arm + torso, right arm + torso) with specific structure induced by the shared joints. Then, we show that we can leverage this structure to efficiently search through the composition of the two roadmaps and largely sidestep the curse of dimensionality. Finally, we run several experiments in a real-world grocery store with this motion planner on a 19 DoF mobile manipulation robot executing a grocery fulfillment task, achieving 0.4s average planning times with 99.9% success rate across more than 2000 motion plans.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Although traditional search methods have been extensively applied, metaheuristic algorithms have gained popularity due to their efficiency and problem-specific heuristics. However, challenges such as premature convergence and lack of solution diversity still hinder their performance in complex scenarios. To address these issues, this paper proposes an Enhanced Multi-Strategy Dwarf Mongoose Optimization (EDMO) algorithm, tailored for three-dimensional UAV trajectory planning in dynamic and obstacle-rich environments. EDMO integrates three novel strategies: (1) a Dynamic Quantum Tunneling Optimization Strategy (DQTOS) to enable particles to probabilistically escape local optima; (2) a Bio-phototactic Dynamic Focusing Search Strategy (BDFSS) inspired by microbial phototaxis for adaptive local refinement; and (3) an Orthogonal Lens Opposition-Based Learning (OLOBL) strategy to enhance global exploration through structured dimensional recombination. EDMO is benchmarked on 39 standard test functions from CEC2017 and CEC2020, outperforming 14 advanced algorithms in convergence speed, robustness, and optimization accuracy. Furthermore, real-world validations on UAV three-dimensional path planning and three engineering design tasks confirm its practical applicability and effectiveness in field robotics missions requiring intelligent, adaptive, and time-efficient planning.

*Shivam Sood,Laukik Nakhwa,Sun Ge,Yuhong Cao,Jin Cheng,Fatemah Zargarbashi,Taerim Yoon,Sungjoon Choi,Stelian Coros,Guillaume Sartoretti*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: APEX是一个即插即用的扩展，用于最先进的运动跟踪算法，它消除了在部署时对参考数据的依赖，提高了样本效率，并减少了参数调整工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的从演示中学习的机器人运动方法在部署时需要大量调整并依赖参考数据，这限制了适应性。

Method: APEX将专家演示直接整合到强化学习（RL）中，通过结合衰减的动作先验，在训练初期引导探索，然后逐渐允许策略独立探索。它还使用多评估器框架来平衡任务性能和运动风格。

Result: APEX能够让单个策略学习到多样化的运动，并在不同地形和速度下迁移参考风格的运动，同时对奖励设计的变化保持鲁棒性。在模拟和Unitree Go2机器人上的实验证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: APEX通过在强化学习训练中利用演示来指导探索，但不强制明确偏向演示，从而使机器人能够更稳定、更高效、更泛化地学习。该方法有望推动引导式强化学习在机器人技能获取方面的应用。

Abstract: Learning natural, animal-like locomotion from demonstrations has become a core paradigm in legged robotics. Despite the recent advancements in motion tracking, most existing methods demand extensive tuning and rely on reference data during deployment, limiting adaptability. We present APEX (Action Priors enable Efficient Exploration), a plug-and-play extension to state-of-the-art motion tracking algorithms that eliminates any dependence on reference data during deployment, improves sample efficiency, and reduces parameter tuning effort. APEX integrates expert demonstrations directly into reinforcement learning (RL) by incorporating decaying action priors, which initially bias exploration toward expert demonstrations but gradually allow the policy to explore independently. This is combined with a multi-critic framework that balances task performance with motion style. Moreover, APEX enables a single policy to learn diverse motions and transfer reference-like styles across different terrains and velocities, while remaining robust to variations in reward design. We validate the effectiveness of our method through extensive experiments in both simulation and on a Unitree Go2 robot. By leveraging demonstrations to guide exploration during RL training, without imposing explicit bias toward them, APEX enables legged robots to learn with greater stability, efficiency, and generalization. We believe this approach paves the way for guidance-driven RL to boost natural skill acquisition in a wide array of robotic tasks, from locomotion to manipulation. Website and code: https://marmotlab.github.io/APEX/.

</details>


### [317] [Decoupling Torque and Stiffness: A Unified Modeling and Control Framework for Antagonistic Artificial Muscles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09104)
*Amirhossein Kazemipour,Robert K. Katzschmann*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 现有的软体驱动器控制器难以在动态接触瞬变中保持独立控制，尽管它们可以实现扭矩-刚度解耦。我们提出了一个统一的框架，可以实时地为各种软体驱动器类型实现独立的扭矩和刚度控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软体驱动器控制器在动态接触瞬变中难以保持独立的扭矩和刚度控制，这限制了它们在软体机器人领域的应用。

Method: 本研究提出了一个统一的框架，包含一个统一的力定律，能够以毫秒级的计算速度模拟各种软体驱动器的物理特性。此外，还设计了一个级联控制器，具有分析逆动力学，以在存在模型误差和干扰的情况下保持解耦。该控制器使用共同收缩/偏置坐标，通过偏置独立调节扭矩，通过共同收缩独立调节刚度，从而模仿生物阻抗策略。

Result: 通过基于仿真的接触实验验证，该框架在模拟中实现了扭矩和刚度控制的独立性。具体而言，在软表面上，执行器能够以比现有策略快200倍的速度稳定下来；在硬表面上，力减小了81%；在与环境的交互中，实现了稳定的交互，而固定策略的稳定性仅为22-54%。

Conclusion: 本框架为实现软体肌肉骨骼系统自适应阻抗控制奠定了基础，有望实现安全的人机交互。

Abstract: Antagonistic soft actuators built from artificial muscles (PAMs, HASELs, DEAs) promise plant-level torque-stiffness decoupling, yet existing controllers for soft muscles struggle to maintain independent control through dynamic contact transients. We present a unified framework enabling independent torque and stiffness commands in real-time for diverse soft actuator types. Our unified force law captures diverse soft muscle physics in a single model with sub-ms computation, while our cascaded controller with analytical inverse dynamics maintains decoupling despite model errors and disturbances. Using co-contraction/bias coordinates, the controller independently modulates torque via bias and stiffness via co-contraction-replicating biological impedance strategies. Simulation-based validation through contact experiments demonstrates maintained independence: 200x faster settling on soft surfaces, 81% force reduction on rigid surfaces, and stable interaction vs 22-54% stability for fixed policies. This framework provides a foundation for enabling musculoskeletal antagonistic systems to execute adaptive impedance control for safe human-robot interaction.

### [318] [Data Assessment for Embodied Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09119)
*Jiahao Xiao,Bowen Yan,Jianbo Zhang,Jia Wang,Chunyi Li,Zhengxue Cheng,Guangtao Zhai*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了两种新的评估和改进数据集的方法：一种是基于统一多模态表示的“多样性熵”，用于量化数据集包含的信息量；另一种是无需训练即可量化数据集可学习性的算法，旨在帮助研究人员在数据集发布后立即评估其质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估数据集的方法（如仅计算任务和场景数量或评估单一模态）无法全面反映多模态数据的多样性，并且通常需要昂贵且耗时的模型训练过程来评估可学习性，缺乏指导性。因此，需要新的、数据驱动的工具来解决这些挑战。

Method: 研究提出了两种工具：1. 统一多模态表示和“多样性熵”，用于量化数据集包含的信息量。2. 首个可解释、数据驱动的算法，用于在不进行模型训练的情况下量化数据集的可学习性。

Result: 在模拟和真实世界的具身数据集上验证了所提出的算法，证明了它们能够提供忠实且可操作的见解，从而能够联合改进数据集的多样性和可学习性。

Conclusion: 这项工作为设计更高质量的数据集奠定了基础，有望推动具身智能的发展。

Abstract: In embodied intelligence, datasets play a pivotal role, serving as both a knowledge repository and a conduit for information transfer. The two most critical attributes of a dataset are the amount of information it provides and how easily this information can be learned by models. However, the multimodal nature of embodied data makes evaluating these properties particularly challenging. Prior work has largely focused on diversity, typically counting tasks and scenes or evaluating isolated modalities, which fails to provide a comprehensive picture of dataset diversity. On the other hand, the learnability of datasets has received little attention and is usually assessed post-hoc through model training, an expensive, time-consuming process that also lacks interpretability, offering little guidance on how to improve a dataset. In this work, we address both challenges by introducing two principled, data-driven tools. First, we construct a unified multimodal representation for each data sample and, based on it, propose diversity entropy, a continuous measure that characterizes the amount of information contained in a dataset. Second, we introduce the first interpretable, data-driven algorithm to efficiently quantify dataset learnability without training, enabling researchers to assess a dataset's learnability immediately upon its release. We validate our algorithm on both simulated and real-world embodied datasets, demonstrating that it yields faithful, actionable insights that enable researchers to jointly improve diversity and learnability. We hope this work provides a foundation for designing higher-quality datasets that advance the development of embodied intelligence.

</details>


### [319] [RGMP: Recurrent Geometric-prior Multimodal Policy for Generalizable Humanoid Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09141)
*Xuetao Li,Wenke Huang,Nengyuan Pan,Kaiyan Zhao,Songhua Yang,Yiming Wang,Mengde Li,Mang Ye,Jifeng Xuan,Miao Li*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前研究过度依赖数据驱动方法，导致在未见场景下泛化能力不足，且训练资源利用效率低下。本研究旨在提出一种新的框架，以解决这些问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为RGMP（Recurrent Geometric-prior Multimodal Policy）的端到端框架，该框架结合了几何先验的语义技能推理和数据高效的视觉-运动控制。具体包括：1. 几何先验技能选择器：将几何归纳偏置注入视觉语言模型，以适应未见场景并生成自适应技能序列。2. 自适应递归高斯网络：将机器人-对象交互参数化为高斯过程的紧凑层级结构，以递归编码多尺度空间关系，实现数据高效的运动合成。

Result: RGMP框架在人形机器人和桌面双臂机器人上的测试均取得了成功。在泛化测试中，任务成功率达到了87%，并且数据效率比现有最先进的模型高出5倍。

Conclusion: RGMP框架通过几何-语义推理和递归高斯适应，实现了优越的跨域泛化能力，克服了现有数据驱动方法的局限性，并在机器人控制任务中展现出高效性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Humanoid robots exhibit significant potential in executing diverse human-level skills. However, current research predominantly relies on data-driven approaches that necessitate extensive training datasets to achieve robust multimodal decision-making capabilities and generalizable visuomotor control. These methods raise concerns due to the neglect of geometric reasoning in unseen scenarios and the inefficient modeling of robot-target relationships within the training data, resulting in significant waste of training resources. To address these limitations, we present the Recurrent Geometric-prior Multimodal Policy (RGMP), an end-to-end framework that unifies geometric-semantic skill reasoning with data-efficient visuomotor control. For perception capabilities, we propose the Geometric-prior Skill Selector, which infuses geometric inductive biases into a vision language model, producing adaptive skill sequences for unseen scenes with minimal spatial common sense tuning. To achieve data-efficient robotic motion synthesis, we introduce the Adaptive Recursive Gaussian Network, which parameterizes robot-object interactions as a compact hierarchy of Gaussian processes that recursively encode multi-scale spatial relationships, yielding dexterous, data-efficient motion synthesis even from sparse demonstrations. Evaluated on both our humanoid robot and desktop dual-arm robot, the RGMP framework achieves 87% task success in generalization tests and exhibits 5x greater data efficiency than the state-of-the-art model. This performance underscores its superior cross-domain generalization, enabled by geometric-semantic reasoning and recursive-Gaussion adaptation.

### [320] [LODESTAR: Degeneracy-Aware LiDAR-Inertial Odometry with Adaptive Schmidt-Kalman Filter and Data Exploitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09142)
*Eungchang Mason Lee,Kevin Christiansen Marsim,Hyun Myung*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: LODESTAR是一种新的激光雷达-惯性里程计（LIO）方法，通过自适应的卡尔曼滤波器和数据利用模块，解决了在长走廊和高空飞行等退化环境下的性能下降问题，提高了精度和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光雷达-惯性里程计（LIO）在机器人领域虽然精度高，但在长走廊和高空飞行等退化环境下，由于激光雷达测量不平衡或稀疏，导致状态估计出现病态问题，性能下降。

Method: LODESTAR包含两个关键模块：退化感知自适应Schmidt-卡尔曼滤波器（DA-ASKF）和退化感知数据利用（DA-DE）。DA-ASKF使用滑动窗口和退化感知滑动模式，自适应地将状态分为活动状态和固定状态，并利用Schmidt-Kalman更新部分优化活动状态。DA-DE根据局部可定位性和雅可比矩阵的条件数，修剪不活跃测量并选择性地利用固定状态的测量。

Result: 实验结果表明，LODESTAR在各种退化条件下，在精度和鲁棒性方面都优于现有的基于激光雷达的里程计方法和退化感知模块。

Conclusion: LODESTAR通过DA-ASKF实现退化感知约束优化，缓解了测量稀疏性；通过DA-DE解决了测量不平衡问题，在退化环境下表现出优越的性能。

Abstract: LiDAR-inertial odometry (LIO) has been widely used in robotics due to its high accuracy. However, its performance degrades in degenerate environments, such as long corridors and high-altitude flights, where LiDAR measurements are imbalanced or sparse, leading to ill-posed state estimation. In this letter, we present LODESTAR, a novel LIO method that addresses these degeneracies through two key modules: degeneracy-aware adaptive Schmidt-Kalman filter (DA-ASKF) and degeneracy-aware data exploitation (DA-DE). DA-ASKF employs a sliding window to utilize past states and measurements as additional constraints. Specifically, it introduces degeneracy-aware sliding modes that adaptively classify states as active or fixed based on their degeneracy level. Using Schmidt-Kalman update, it partially optimizes active states while preserving fixed states. These fixed states influence the update of active states via their covariances, serving as reference anchors--akin to a lodestar. Additionally, DA-DE prunes less-informative measurements from active states and selectively exploits measurements from fixed states, based on their localizability contribution and the condition number of the Jacobian matrix. Consequently, DA-ASKF enables degeneracy-aware constrained optimization and mitigates measurement sparsity, while DA-DE addresses measurement imbalance. Experimental results show that LODESTAR outperforms existing LiDAR-based odometry methods and degeneracy-aware modules in terms of accuracy and robustness under various degenerate conditions.

</details>


### [321] [Unveiling the Impact of Data and Model Scaling on High-Level Control for Humanoid Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09241)
*Yuxi Wei,Zirui Wang,Kangning Yin,Yue Hu,Jingbo Wang,Siheng Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究介绍了Humanoid-Union数据集和SCHUR框架，以解决机器人学习中的数据扩展瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器人学习数据扩展面临瓶颈，而人类视频和运动数据丰富，但如何有效利用这些数据进行机器人学习仍是未解决的问题。

Method: 研究人员创建了一个名为Humanoid-Union的大规模数据集，其中包含260多小时的人形机器人运动数据，并带有语义标注。他们还提出了一个名为SCHUR的可扩展学习框架，用于探索大规模数据对机器人高级控制的影响。

Result: SCHUR框架在数据和模型扩展方面都实现了高质量的机器人运动生成和强大的文本-运动对齐，与现有方法相比，MPJPE重建提高了37%，FID对齐提高了25%。

Abstract: Data scaling has long remained a critical bottleneck in robot learning. For humanoid robots, human videos and motion data are abundant and widely available, offering a free and large-scale data source. Besides, the semantics related to the motions enable modality alignment and high-level robot control learning. However, how to effectively mine raw video, extract robot-learnable representations, and leverage them for scalable learning remains an open problem. To address this, we introduce Humanoid-Union, a large-scale dataset generated through an autonomous pipeline, comprising over 260 hours of diverse, high-quality humanoid robot motion data with semantic annotations derived from human motion videos. The dataset can be further expanded via the same pipeline. Building on this data resource, we propose SCHUR, a scalable learning framework designed to explore the impact of large-scale data on high-level control in humanoid robots. Experimental results demonstrate that SCHUR achieves high robot motion generation quality and strong text-motion alignment under data and model scaling, with 37\% reconstruction improvement under MPJPE and 25\% alignment improvement under FID comparing with previous methods. Its effectiveness is further validated through deployment in real-world humanoid robot.

### [322] [UMIGen: A Unified Framework for Egocentric Point Cloud Generation and Cross-Embodiment Robotic Imitation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09302)
*Yan Huang,Shoujie Li,Xingting Li,Wenbo Ding*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出UMIGen框架，包括Cloud-UMI设备（无需视觉SLAM，记录点云观察-动作对）和可见性感知优化机制（扩展DemoGen，处理以自我为中心的3D观察）。

Abstract: Data-driven robotic learning faces an obvious dilemma: robust policies demand large-scale, high-quality demonstration data, yet collecting such data remains a major challenge owing to high operational costs, dependence on specialized hardware, and the limited spatial generalization capability of current methods. The Universal Manipulation Interface (UMI) relaxes the strict hardware requirements for data collection, but it is restricted to capturing only RGB images of a scene and omits the 3D geometric information on which many tasks rely. Inspired by DemoGen, we propose UMIGen, a unified framework that consists of two key components: (1) Cloud-UMI, a handheld data collection device that requires no visual SLAM and simultaneously records point cloud observation-action pairs; and (2) a visibility-aware optimization mechanism that extends the DemoGen pipeline to egocentric 3D observations by generating only points within the camera's field of view. These two components enable efficient data generation that aligns with real egocentric observations and can be directly transferred across different robot embodiments without any post-processing. ### [323] [SPIDER: Scalable Physics-Informed Dexterous Retargeting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09484)
*Chaoyi Pan,Changhao Wang,Haozhi Qi,Zixi Liu,Homanga Bharadhwaj,Akash Sharma,Tingfan Wu,Guanya Shi,Jitendra Malik,Francois Hogan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SPIDER框架利用人类动作数据，通过物理模拟和强化学习，生成机器人可执行的动态轨迹，解决了机器人数据稀缺和动作不匹配问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人控制（尤其是人形机器人和灵巧手）需要大量数据，但机器人特定数据的收集成本高昂。而人类动作数据（如动作捕捉、视频、VR）相对丰富，可用于弥补数据不足。然而，由于具身差异和动态信息（如力矩）缺失，人类演示不能直接用于机器人。SPIDER旨在解决此问题。

Method: SPIDER是一个基于物理的重定向框架，利用大规模的物理模拟和课程式虚拟接触引导，对仅包含运动学的人类演示进行转换和增强，生成动态可行的机器人轨迹。人类演示提供任务的全局结构和目标，而物理模拟则用于确保动态可行性和正确的接触序列。

Result: SPIDER框架能够处理9种不同的人形/灵巧手具身和6个数据集，与标准采样方法相比，成功率提高了18%。与强化学习基线方法相比，SPIDER的速度提高了10倍，并成功生成了240万帧的动态可行机器人数据集，用于策略学习。该方法能够处理不同质量的数据，并生成多样化的高质量数据。

Conclusion: SPIDER是一个通用的、基于物理的重定向方法，能够有效地将人类演示转换为机器人可执行的、动态可行的轨迹，从而解决数据稀缺问题，并为高效的策略学习（如强化学习）提供支持。

Abstract: Learning dexterous and agile policy for humanoid and dexterous hand control requires large-scale demonstrations, but collecting robot-specific data is prohibitively expensive. In contrast, abundant human motion data is readily available from motion capture, videos, and virtual reality, which could help address the data scarcity problem. However, due to the embodiment gap and missing dynamic information like force and torque, these demonstrations cannot be directly executed on robots. To bridge this gap, we propose Scalable Physics-Informed DExterous Retargeting (SPIDER), a physics-based retargeting framework to transform and augment kinematic-only human demonstrations to dynamically feasible robot trajectories at scale. Our key insight is that human demonstrations should provide global task structure and objective, while large-scale physics-based sampling with curriculum-style virtual contact guidance should refine trajectories to ensure dynamical feasibility and correct contact sequences. SPIDER scales across diverse 9 humanoid/dexterous hand embodiments and 6 datasets, improving success rates by 18% compared to standard sampling, while being 10X faster than reinforcement learning (RL) baselines, and enabling the generation of a 2.4M frames dynamic-feasible robot dataset for policy learning. As a universal physics-based retargeting method, SPIDER can work with diverse quality data and generate diverse and high-quality data to enable efficient policy learning with methods like RL.

</details>


### [324] [WMPO: World Model-based Policy Optimization for Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09515)
*Fangqi Zhu,Zhengyang Yan,Zicong Hong,Quanxin Shou,Xiao Ma,Song Guo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: WMPO是一个基于世界模型的策略优化框架，用于在机器人操作领域实现无需与真实环境交互的强化学习，提高了样本效率、性能和泛化能力，并展现出自我修正等新兴行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在机器人操作方面潜力巨大，但依赖专家演示，难以从失败中学习和自我修正。强化学习（RL）可以通过与物理环境的交互进行自我改进，但实际操作中样本复杂度高。本研究旨在解决这些问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为WMPO（World-Model-based Policy Optimization）的框架，该框架基于世界模型，可以在不与真实环境交互的情况下进行视觉-语言-动作（VLA）的强化学习。与现有的隐变量世界模型不同，WMPO关注像素级预测，使“想象”的轨迹与通过网络规模图像预训练的VLA特征对齐。关键在于，WMPO支持策略进行在线GRPO，相比常用的离线方法，性能更强。

Result: 大量模拟和真实机器人实验证明，WMPO在提高样本效率、整体性能、展现出自我修正等新兴行为以及泛化和终身学习能力方面均有显著提升。

Conclusion: WMPO框架通过像素级预测和在线GRPO，有效解决了VLA强化学习中的样本效率和性能问题，并实现了机器人操作中的自我修正、泛化和终身学习能力。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown strong potential for general-purpose robotic manipulation, but their reliance on expert demonstrations limits their ability to learn from failures and perform self-corrections. Reinforcement learning (RL) addresses these through self-improving interactions with the physical environment, but suffers from high sample complexity on real robots. We introduce World-Model-based Policy Optimization (WMPO), a principled framework for on-policy VLA RL without interacting with the real environment. In contrast to widely used latent world models, WMPO focuses on pixel-based predictions that align the "imagined" trajectories with the VLA features pretrained with web-scale images. Crucially, WMPO enables the policy to perform on-policy GRPO that provides stronger performance than the often-used off-policy methods. Extensive experiments in both simulation and real-robot settings demonstrate that WMPO (i) substantially improves sample efficiency, (ii) achieves stronger overall performance, (iii) exhibits emergent behaviors such as self-correction, and (iv) demonstrates robust generalization and lifelong learning capabilities.

</details>

*Runhao Li,Wenkai Guo,Zhenyu Wu,Changyuan Wang,Haoyuan Deng,Zhenyu Weng,Yap-Peng Tan,Ziwei Wang*

Method: MAP-VLA框架通过构建包含任务阶段信息的记忆库（以可学习的软提示形式），并在任务执行时通过轨迹相似性匹配检索相关记忆，然后将其动态集成到VLA模型中来增强动作生成。

Result: MAP-VLA在长程任务的模拟基准测试中提高了7.0%的性能，在真实机器人评估中提高了25.0%，优于现有技术。
